    <div class="main-discussion-guidelines discussion-guidelines">
    
    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Answer more questions</div>
    <p>
        Visit <a href="/computing/computer-programming/d">Community Questions</a>
        to answer new questions in
        <a href="/computing/computer-programming/d">Computer programming</a>.
    </p>
    <br>
    

    

    

    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Discuss the site</div>
        <p>
            View <a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/hc/communities/public/topics">general discussions about Khan Academy</a>.
        </p>
    <br>
    

    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Flag inappropriate posts</div>

    <p>
        Here are posts to avoid making. If you do encounter them, flag them for attention from our Guardians.
    </p>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">abuse</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>disrespectful or offensive</li>
        
        <li>an advertisement</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">not helpful</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>low quality</li>
        
        <li>not about the video topic</li>
        
        <li>contentious posts about politics, religion/atheism, or personal issues</li>
        
        <li>soliciting votes or seeking badges</li>
        
        <li>a homework question</li>
        
        <li>a duplicate answer</li>
        
        <li>repeatedly making the same post</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">wrong category</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>a tip or thanks in Questions</li>
        
        <li>a question in Tips &amp; Thanks</li>
        
        <li>an answer that should be its own question</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">about the site</div>
    <ul>
        
            <li>
                a question about Khan Academy
                <div class="discussion-guidelines-link">(<a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/">Visit our FAQ</a>)</div>
            </li>
        
        <li>a post about badges</li>
        
            <li>
                a technical problem with the site
                <div class="discussion-guidelines-link">(<a href="http://khanacademy.org/reportissue?type=Defect">Report a problem</a>)</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                a request for <a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/hc/communities/public/topics/200136634-Feature-Requests">features</a>
            </li>
        
    </ul>
</div>

    (function() {

        // If their computer clock is off by more than a day, complain
        // about that too (causes SSL problems)
        if (Math.abs(KA.currentServerTime() - new Date() / 1000) >= 60 * 60 * 24 &&

    <script>
    (function() {
        // If we arrived via a Facebook callback, it might have appended #_=_
        // to our URL. This can confuse our Backbone routers, so get rid of it.
        // http://stackoverflow.com/questions/7131909/facebook-callback-appends-to-return-url
        if (window.location.hash === "#_=_") {
            if (history.replaceState) {
                history.replaceState(null, null,
                        window.location.href.split("#")[0]);
            } else {
                window.location.hash = "";
            }
        }
    })();
    </script>

    <div class="main-discussion-guidelines discussion-guidelines">
    
    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Answer more questions</div>
    <p>
        Visit <a href="/computing/computer-programming/d">Community Questions</a>
        to answer new questions in
        <a href="/computing/computer-programming/d">Computer programming</a>.
    </p>
    <br>
    

    

    

    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Discuss the site</div>
        <p>
            View <a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/hc/communities/public/topics">general discussions about Khan Academy</a>.
        </p>
    <br>
    

    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Flag inappropriate posts</div>

    <p>
        Here are posts to avoid making. If you do encounter them, flag them for attention from our Guardians.
    </p>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">abuse</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>disrespectful or offensive</li>
        
        <li>an advertisement</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">not helpful</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>low quality</li>
        
        <li>not about the video topic</li>
        
        <li>contentious posts about politics, religion/atheism, or personal issues</li>
        
        <li>soliciting votes or seeking badges</li>
        
        <li>a homework question</li>
        
        <li>a duplicate answer</li>
        
        <li>repeatedly making the same post</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">wrong category</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>a tip or thanks in Questions</li>
        
        <li>a question in Tips &amp; Thanks</li>
        
        <li>an answer that should be its own question</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">about the site</div>
    <ul>
        
            <li>
                a question about Khan Academy
                <div class="discussion-guidelines-link">(<a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/">Visit our FAQ</a>)</div>
            </li>
        
        <li>a post about badges</li>
        
            <li>
                a technical problem with the site
                <div class="discussion-guidelines-link">(<a href="http://khanacademy.org/reportissue?type=Defect">Report a problem</a>)</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                a request for <a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/hc/communities/public/topics/200136634-Feature-Requests">features</a>
            </li>
        
    </ul>
</div>

    (function() {
        var KA = KAdefine.require("./javascript/shared-package/ka.js");
        // If their computer clock is off by more than a day, complain
        // about that too (causes SSL problems)
        if (Math.abs(KA.currentServerTime() - new Date() / 1000) >= 60 * 60 * 24 &&
                document.getElementById("inaccurate-clock-warning")) {

    <script>
    (function() {
        // If we arrived via a Facebook callback, it might have appended #_=_
        // to our URL. This can confuse our Backbone routers, so get rid of it.
        // http://stackoverflow.com/questions/7131909/facebook-callback-appends-to-return-url
        if (window.location.hash === "#_=_") {
            if (history.replaceState) {
                history.replaceState(null, null,
                        window.location.href.split("#")[0]);
            } else {
                window.location.hash = "";
            }
        }
    })();
    </script>

    <div class="main-discussion-guidelines discussion-guidelines">
    
    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Answer more questions</div>
    <p>
        Visit <a href="/computing/computer-programming/d">Community Questions</a>
        to answer new questions in
        <a href="/computing/computer-programming/d">Computer programming</a>.
    </p>
    <br>
    

    

    

    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Discuss the site</div>
        <p>
            View <a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/hc/communities/public/topics">general discussions about Khan Academy</a>.
        </p>
    <br>
    

    <div class="discussion-guidelines-header">Flag inappropriate posts</div>

    <p>
        Here are posts to avoid making. If you do encounter them, flag them for attention from our Guardians.
    </p>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">abuse</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>disrespectful or offensive</li>
        
        <li>an advertisement</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">not helpful</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>low quality</li>
        
        <li>not about the video topic</li>
        
        <li>contentious posts about politics, religion/atheism, or personal issues</li>
        
        <li>soliciting votes or seeking badges</li>
        
        <li>a homework question</li>
        
        <li>a duplicate answer</li>
        
        <li>repeatedly making the same post</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">wrong category</div>
    <ul>
        
        <li>a tip or thanks in Questions</li>
        
        <li>a question in Tips &amp; Thanks</li>
        
        <li>an answer that should be its own question</li>
    </ul>

    
    <div class="discussion-guidelines-subheader">about the site</div>
    <ul>
        
            <li>
                a question about Khan Academy
                <div class="discussion-guidelines-link">(<a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/">Visit our FAQ</a>)</div>
            </li>
        
        <li>a post about badges</li>
        
            <li>
                a technical problem with the site
                <div class="discussion-guidelines-link">(<a href="http://khanacademy.org/reportissue?type=Defect">Report a problem</a>)</div>
            </li>
            <li>
                a request for <a href="https://khanacademy.zendesk.com/hc/communities/public/topics/200136634-Feature-Requests">features</a>
            </li>
        
    </ul>
</div>

    (function() {
        var KA = KAdefine.require("./javascript/shared-package/ka.js");
        // If their computer clock is off by more than a day, complain
        // about that too (causes SSL problems)
        if (Math.abs(KA.currentServerTime() - new Date() / 1000) >= 60 * 60 * 24 &&
                document.getElementById("inaccurate-clock-warning")) {

    <script>
    (function() {
        // If we arrived via a Facebook callback, it might have appended #_=_
        // to our URL. This can confuse our Backbone routers, so get rid of it.
        // http://stackoverflow.com/questions/7131909/facebook-callback-appends-to-return-url
        if (window.location.hash === "#_=_") {
            if (history.replaceState) {
                history.replaceState(null, null,
                        window.location.href.split("#")[0]);
            } else {
                window.location.hash = "";
            }
        }
    })();
    </script>
